## Idea

The orbit of a point `x` for a permutation `f` is the set of point obtained by iterating `f` on `x`.

## Properties

### For type equipped with a counting, orbits of permutations are finite

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6673" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6680" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6680" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="6684" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6685" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6685" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6687" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6689" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6694" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6696" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6697" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6697" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6699" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6701" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6704" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6685" class="Bound">l</a><a id="6705" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6707" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6708" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6708" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="6711" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6713" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1759" class="Function">count</a> <a id="6719" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6697" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6722" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6723" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6723" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6727" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1210" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="6731" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6697" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6732" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6734" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6735" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6735" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="6737" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6739" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6697" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6740" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="6744" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="6755" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6755" class="Function">two-points-iterate-Fin</a> <a id="6778" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6784" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6788" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2085" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6792" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6793" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1478" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="6800" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6801" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1887" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="6826" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6708" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="6828" class="Symbol">)))</a>

### For finite types, the number of orbits-permutation of a permutation is finite.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="17633" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="17640" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17640" class="Module">_</a>

        <a id="25786" href="foundation.decidable-types.html#1905" class="Function">is-decidable</a>
          <a id="25809" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25811" href="foundation.equivalence-classes.html#3224" class="Function">type-class-large-set-quotient</a> <a id="25841" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17731" class="Function">same-orbits-permutation</a> <a id="25865" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#25615" class="Bound">T2</a> <a id="25868" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#25673" class="Bound">t1</a><a id="25870" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25872" class="Symbol">→</a>

      <a id="39301" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#38901" class="Function">lemma2</a> <a id="39308" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#39308" class="Bound">pa</a> <a id="39311" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39312" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#1262" class="InductiveConstructor">inr</a> <a id="39316" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#39316" class="Bound">p</a><a id="39317" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="39319" class="Symbol">=</a>

          <a id="49105" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#49105" class="Function">is-successor-k1</a> <a id="49121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="49123" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1848" class="Function">is-successor-ℕ</a> <a id="49138" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="49139" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="49143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="49144" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#44909" class="Function">minimal-element-iterate-2-a-b</a> <a id="49174" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#46619" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="49176" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#46621" class="Bound">pa</a><a id="49178" class="Symbol">))</a>

              <a id="79483" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="79485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="79486" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a>

            <a id="84154" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="84156" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="84158" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#84158" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="84160" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="84162" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#26409" class="Function">sign-permutation-orbit</a> <a id="84185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84186" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1887" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="84211" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#82898" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="84213" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="84215" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84216" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#575" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="84221" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#82887" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="84223" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84224" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2096" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="84240" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84241" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1956" class="Function">equiv-count</a> <a id="84253" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#82898" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="84255" class="Symbol">)))</a>
              <a id="84273" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84274" href="finite-group-theory.transpositions.html#10077" class="Function">permutation-list-transpositions</a> <a id="84306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84307" href="univalent-combinatorics.lists.html#2210" class="InductiveConstructor">cons</a> <a id="84312" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#84158" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="84314" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#83503" class="Bound">li</a><a id="84316" class="Symbol">)))</a>
            <a id="84332" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="84334" class="Argument">x</a> <a id="84336" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="84338" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-decidable-subtypes.html#10169" class="Function">standard-2-Element-Decidable-Subtype</a> <a id="84375" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84376" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#5721" class="Function">has-decidable-equality-count</a> <a id="84405" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#82898" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="84407" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="84409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84410" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="84414" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84415" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="84419" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84420" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="84424" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#84530" class="Function">two-elements-t</a><a id="84438" class="Symbol">)))}</a>
            <a id="84455" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="84457" class="Argument">y</a> <a id="84459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="84461" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#83501" class="Bound">t</a><a id="84462" class="Symbol">}</a>
            <a id="84476" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="84478" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="84482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84483" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="84487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84488" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="84492" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#84530" class="Function">two-elements-t</a><a id="84506" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
      <a id="84518" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="84530" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#84530" class="Function">two-elements-t</a> <a id="84545" class="Symbol">:</a>
        <a id="84555" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="84557" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#82887" class="Bound">X</a> <a <a id="84603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="84604" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-decidable-subtypes.html#10169" class="Function">standard-2-Element-Decidable-Subtype</a> <a id="84641"
